IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [a] or [b].

You MUST choose either [a] or [b]. Your response must be ONLY [a] or [b] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [a] or [b].

You MUST choose either [a] or [b]. Your response must be ONLY [a] or [b] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [a] or [b].

You MUST choose either [a] or [b]. Your response must be ONLY [a] or [b] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.
